## String References

- **10724**: Pyopyoroon peers intently at <Player>!
- **11648**: Kilusha glares at you.
- **11737**: What will you ask about? [Alexandrite gems[./ (done).]/Wyrmseeker of Areuhat[./ (done).]/Assault memoires[./ (done).]/Holy relics[./ (done).]/No explanations required.]
- **11793**: You receive five bound volumes containing blank pages.
- **11795**: What are these "assault memoires"? [Quit./How to use the memoires./Recording $1./Recording $2./Recording $3./Recording $4./Recording $5.]
- **11796**: Trade the blank memoire to the Rune of Release which appears following successful completion of an Assault mission. This will result in the relevant data being recorded to the pages within.
- **11797**: Completion of a memoire requires a player to clear all Assault missions spanning ranks Private Second Class to First Lieutenant in all relevant areas excepting Nyzul Isle, for which no memoire exists.
- **11798**: Loss or disposal of a memoire will result in the loss of any recorded data without the possibility of recovery. Please exercise caution in this respect.
- **11799**: In the event of a lost memoire, the option to acquire a new one will appear on this menu NPC menu.
- **11800**: This quest cannot be accepted while in possession of an outdated memoire. You will be required to dispose of the old memoire before taking on the quest.
